ZHES YANG YANG BSNGAGS BRJOD MDZAD, MTHAR YAB SRAS 'BRAL MI PHOD

PHYOGS DANG MA 'BREL BA'I BRGYUD PA GTZANG NGES THUGS TSIM PA
ZHIG MA RNYED PAR YOD PA LA, BYA KHYUNG GI KHRIR PHEBS SKABS,
CHA HAR PHYOGS NAS CHOS RJES BLO BZANG BKRA SHIS MJAL DU

PEBS PA DANG GSUNG 'PHROS GNANG BAS LUNG RGYUN KHUNGS BTZUN YOD
PAR GZIGS TE, SLAR BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL DU BKA' 'GYUR GYI LUNG ZHIG
BYED DGOS KYI BKA' PHEBS, DE DON BZHIN LO SNGA MA'I MJUG TU
KHONG CHED GTAD KYIS BYON

PAR BSU BA KHAL RTA SOGS DANG DGON PAR BZHUGS RING DPON GA-YOG
KUN LA YO BYAD GANG DGOS KYI MTHUN RKYEN PHUL DU PHYIN PA
BSGRUBS, DANG POR SPRUL SKU DGE BSHES SOGS SNYAN GSAN 'BUL MI
SUM CU TZAM BYUNG STE, BLA MAS KYANG

LUNG GI MGO TSUGS RTZIS GNANG SKABS, DA DUNG NYAN MKHAN KHO
'BYOR MA BYUNG GSUNGS TE, RI KHROD PA RAB RGYAS RANG YUL NA YOD
PA LA BKA' SHOG NAN CAN BSKUR NAS 'BOD PA GNANG, DE NAS LUNG GI
MGO BYAMS CHEN RAB GNAS

KYI SBYOR BA DANG PHYOGS MTSUNGS SU TSUGS RGYU'I BKOD KHYAB
STZAL, DE'I DGONGS GZHI NI RJE BLA MA MCHOG GI THUGS MKHYEN
BRTZE'I YE SHES KYIS 'GRO KUN NAM YANG MI GTONG BAR 'DU 'BRAL
MED PAR RTAG TU 'GROGS KYANG, THUN MONG GDUL

BYA'I SNANG NGOR GZUGS SKU'I BKOD PA NYE BAR BSDUS TE, SKU'I
ZHAL SKYIN DU BYAMS CHEN MTHONG BA DON LDAN DANG, GSUNG GI DOD
POR RGYAL PA'I LUNG GI BSTAN PA CHA TSANG BA'I BYIN RLABS KYI
RGYUN MA NYAMS BA ZHIG GNANG BZHED PA GONG MA

@230A *, ,CHAG GO, ,DER MA ZANG SNGA SOR BOD DU BZHUGS SKABS
YONGS 'DZIN YE SHES RGYAL MTSAN DANG BKA' MCHID GNANG SKABS SHIG
DED KYIS BOD SNGA PHYI'I MKHAS PA THAMS CAD KYI LEGS BSHAD CHA

TSANG BA BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL DU 'BYOR BA ZHIG BYED BSAM PA YOD
GSUNGS PA YANG 'DI DANG GNAD GCIG STE, RGYAL BA'I BKA' DANG,
'PHAGS BOD KYI BSTAN BCOS MA LUS PA'I GLEGS BAM TZAM ZHIG BZHUGS
NA YANG, DE'I BYIN RLABS

LA BRTEN NAS BSHAD SGRUB KYI BSTAN PA 'PHEL RGYAS SU 'GRO BA
DANG, DGON PAR PHYAG DANG SKOR BA LAN GCIG BYAS BA TZAM GYIS
KYANG DE THAMS CAD LA 'BREL THOGS PA SOGS DGOS PA PHAS GYI MI
KHYAB PAS, RDZA BUM ZHIG TU 'BRA SNA KHA SHAS RE BLUGS

PA LA SA'I BCUD DU BTAGS PA DANG MI 'DRA BAR, GNAS KYIS GANG ZAG
BYIN GYIS RLOB NUS PA'I MTHU DANG LDAN PAR BSGRUBS BAR SHES PAR
GYIS LA BKA' DRIN RJES SU DRAN PAR PHYOS SHIG ,CHOS NYAN PA'I
GRANGS DER MKHAS PA'I DBANG PO CHOS

RGYUN SPEL NUS PA DU MA YOD KYANG, KUN GYI NANG NAS RAB RGYAS LA
CHED GNYER GYIS BKA' PHEBS PA NI, DE PHYIN GYI LO BDUN PO 'DI'I
BAR DU YANG KHONG GIS GDAN SA 'DI DANG, SKU 'BUM BYAMS PA GLING,
CO NE'I PHYOGS SOGS SU BKA'

'GYUR RGYI LUNG TSAR LNGA TZAM BYAS TE, RGYAL BA'I 'PHRIN LAS
SPEL BA'I BKA' 'GYUR BA CHEN BO ZHIG TU SONG BA 'DI NYID SGRIB
BA MED PA'I YE SHES KYIS MNGON SUM DU GZIGS PAR SNANG, BKA'
'GYUR BA BLO BZANG BKRA SHIS KYIS ZHUS

@230B NGOR LUNG GI BRGYUD BDE BA SHIG LJAGS RTZOM GNANG YANG
SBYAR BYANG MA BTAB BAS, GANG BSKYAR GYIS ZHUS PA LA MDZAD BYANG
SLAR 'DRI ZHES GNANG BA NI GDAN SA 'DIR BKA' RTZOM GYI THAM YIN
PAS SLAD KYI RTEN 'DREL LA DGONGS PAR MNGON

GSUM PA'I NYEN DRUG LA BYA KHYUNG DU CHIBS BSGYUR SKABS DGON
PA'I MTHA' NAS PHEBS BYAMS PHYIR BSKOR TE DGON PAR GZIGS PA SOGS
RGYUN LDAN DANG MI 'DRA BZHIG GNANG, BZHI BA'I SMON LAM GYI RIL
BYA KHYUNG DU BZUGS TE LUGS

GNYIS GYIS RE BA BSKANGS SHING, RGYUD PA BLA MA GDAN ZUR GNYIS,
BDE YANGS ZHABS DRUNG, DKA' BUG ZHABS DRUNG SOGS DON GNYER CAN
DU MAL 'DOD SBYAR GYI CHOS DKAL 'GA' ZHIG STZAL, RIM GYIS PHYAG
BTEG STE LNGA

BA'I TSES GSUM LA SGO MCHU TSAN KHAR 'BYON, DGE 'DUN GUNG TSANG
NAS AEM CHI RGYAL MTSAN BOS TE GSOL SMAN DRANGS SHING, MDUN
PHRAG GCIG TU CHAB TSAN GYI 'PHROD BRTEN GNANG BAS CUNG ZAD PHAN
NGE DOD PA BYANG, DE'I SENG

BZANG RGYAL MTSAN RNAM GNYIS SOGS RI KHROD PA BCU SKOR LA RDO
RJE 'JIGS BYED CHEN PO'I BSKYED RDZOGS GNYIS KYI KHRID MAN DAG
DU MA'I THAB GNAD DANG BCAS PA STZAL, PHYIR

LAM SHUG CHU RI KHROD DU GDAN DRANGS PAR 'JIGS BYED BCU GSUM
MA'I DBANG STA GON DANG BCAS PA GNANG SKABS NAM MKHA'I NGOS
THAMS CAD 'JA' TSON BLUM PO DU MAS KHYAB PA SOGS LTAS DE MTSAR
BA MANG DU BYUNG BAS KUN YA MTSAN DU

BA BLO BZANG RGYAL MTSAN DANG NGAG DBANG NYI MA GNYIS LA DPA'
GCIG DANG, ZHI KHRO SGRAGS SGRUB KYI LJAGS LUNG GNANG, BDE CHEN
DU SER SKYA LNGA BRGYA SKOR LA

DNGOS STA 'BREL MA BYAS TE KUN RIG RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD KYI
DBANG CHEN STZAL NAS NGAN SONG GI SGO 'PHAR DAM DU BCAD, LAM GYI
YI KHYIM MTHA' DAG GIS RANG 'BYOR DANG BSTUN PA'I BSNYEN BKUR
ZHUS PA THAMS CAD BRTZE BA CHEN POS RJES SU

PHYAG MCHOD, SMAN GYI RGYUD BZHI SOGS 'DOD MOS BZHIN GYI CHOS
BKA' CI RIGS GNANG, KHA TI KHA BA SMAN PA

DKON MCHOG YAR 'PHEL GYIS ZHUS NGOR BRGYAD STONG BA'I LJAGS LUNG
GNANG SKABS PHYAG GA-YAS PA'I MTHE BONG GIS RKAN PHUG TU YANG
YANG REG PAR CHOS NYAN PA 'GA' ZHIG GIS BLTAS BAS, AA 'OD KYI

BYE BRAG BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA DANG BCAS,

@231B SEMS BSKYED KYI CHOG RGYAS PAR GNANG ZHING, DA SKAL BA

KYI SKABS SU MYONG BA LA BSKOR NAS BLO 'CHUN NGES PA GEGS SEL
BOGS 'BYIN SOGS KYI MAN NGAG DANG BCAS NYAMS SU BLANG BDE BA
DANG, DBANG RJES GNANG SOGS LA THOR

DNGOS RJES GSUM GYI CHO GA PHYAG LEN THAMS CAD ZUR CUNG ZAD TZAM
YANG MA NYAMS SHING LHA SNGAGS KYI CHE BA YID 'GYUR NGES DANG,
SKABS THOB KYI DMIGS RIM BRDA 'PHROD NGES PA SOGS GNANG BAS MDO
SNGAGS RIG GNAS GANG GI SKABS SU YANG

'CHAD TSUL 'PHRAN PA'I ZLA DANG BRAL BA ZHIG YOD LA, RTZOD PA NI
MKHAS PA 'JUG PA'I SGO LAS, RGOL BA RNAM GNYIS RANG RANG GI
,GRUB MTHA' BA ZUNG NAS RTZOD PA NI, ,SNGON GYI MKHAS PA RNAMS
KYI LUGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTA MA 'PHAGS

BA'I YUL DU PHYI NANG GI PAndI TA RNAMS RTZOD BA'I TSE RGOL PHYI
RGOL DBANG PO GSUM BYAS TE GRUB MTHA' BYINGS LAS BRTZAMS PA'I
RTZOD PA LTA BU NI, 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM GSUM DU PHYE BA'I RTZOD
PA'I YON TAN YIN LA, GZHUNG KHOL BUR BTON NAS

DGAG SGRUB BYED PA LTA BU BSHAD BA'I SKABS KYI RTZOD PAR GSUNGS
NA YANG, BOD 'DIR PHYI MA TZAM LAS SBA MA'I SROL CHER MA BYUNG
NGO, ,'ON KYANG RJE BLA MA 'DIS NI SNGAR GRVA SAR BZHUGS PA'I
SKABS SOGS SU SMRA BA'I DBANG PHYUG CHEN POR GRAGS PA

@236A *, ,DU MA DANG RTZOD PA GNANG BA'I TSE RJE 'DI'I RIGS PA'I
RNAM 'GYUR LA SUS KYANG 'GRAN DU MED PA'I TSUL THOR BU ZHIG GONG
DU SONG ZIN LA, PHYIS SU YANG BRGAL BTAG GI RIGS PA'I GSANG TSIG
PHRA MO RTZOD

BZHIN PA RNAMS KYIS KYANG NGES DKA' BA MTHA' DAG NAM YANG BSNYEL
BA MED PAR THUGS LA NGES SHING, GZHAN GYIS SGRUB BYED PA RGYA
STONG BKOD PA LAS KYANG RJE 'DIS RIGS PA'I SGO RE RE PHYE BA DE
RNAM DPYOD CAN RNAMS LA BLO'I 'DUG PA RGYAS PA'I

PHUL STER TSABS CHE BA DANG, DGAG SGRUB BRKYANGS TE MDZAD SKABS
RIGS BA SNGA MA SNGA MA LAS PHYI MA 'PHRUL CHE BA SHA STAG GI
SGO NAS MTHAR PHA ROL PO LAN GYIS PHONGS TE MI SMRA PA'I BRTUL
ZHUGS LA GNAS PA MA GTOGS, NYID KYI SPOBS PA

YONGS SU GTUGS NAS RTZOD PA MTSAMS BYAS PA ZHIG YUL DUS GANG DU
YANG BYUNG TSUL SUS KYANG BSNYAD DU MED DO, ,DER MA ZAD SHIN TU
PHRA ZHING MDZANGS BAS BLO GROS CAN ZHIG GIS LEGS PAR BRTAGS NA,
GSUNG RAB KYI DGONGS DON

'CHAD PA'I SKABS KYI GSUNG ZUR RE RE LA YANG, RTZOD RIGS LAS,
SGRUB BA'I YAN LAG MI BRJOD CING, ,SKYON MI BRJOD PA GNYIS PO
DAG ,TSAR BCAD PA YI GNAS YIN GYI, ,GSUNGS PA LTA BU'I RANG GI
DAM BCA'I SGRUB BYED KYI

NUS BA MTHON ZHING, ZLOG ZLA KHEGS MI NUS PA DANG, THA NA RTAGS
KYI TSER MA DBYUNG DGOS BA MA BSAL BA LTA BU'I SKYON GYIS SPAGS
PA NAM YANG MI SRID PAS, THAL DANG PHYIR SOGS SBYAR MA SBYAR
